\"The Grafana datasource plugin query path follows a layered architecture from HTTP entry point to backend datasource execution:\\n\\n## HTTP Request Entry Point\\nThe query request enters at **pkg/api/ds_query.go** via the `QueryMetricsV2` endpoint (POST /ds/query). This HTTP handler can also route to the new query service API at `/apis/query.grafana.app/v0alpha1/namespaces/{ns}/query` when the `QueryServiceRewrite` feature flag is enabled.\\n\\n## Query Service Layer\\n**pkg/services/query/query.go** contains the `ServiceImpl.QueryData` method that serves as the main query dispatcher. It:\\n- Validates datasources and queries\\n- Routes expression queries to the expression service (`pkg/expr/service.go`)\\n- Executes concurrent queries across multiple datasources\\n- Handles backend query execution via the plugin client\\n\\n## DataSource Proxy\\n**pkg/services/datasourceproxy/datasourceproxy.go** provides proxy functionality at `ProxyDatasourceRequestWithUID` and `ProxyDatasourceRequestWithID`. This service:\\n- Retrieves datasource configurations\\n- Validates datasource access permissions\\n- Locates the appropriate plugin\\n- Forwards requests to the plugin execution layer\\n\\n## Plugin Execution Layer\\nThe plugin client and manager implement the query dispatch:\\n\\n1. **pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go** (`Service.QueryData`): The plugin manager client routes requests to the correct plugin instance via the plugin registry\\n\\n2. **pkg/plugins/plugins.go** (`Plugin.QueryData`): The plugin wrapper retrieves the actual backend plugin client and delegates the query\\n\\n3. **pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/grpc_plugin.go** (`grpcPlugin.QueryData`): For gRPC-based plugins, establishes connection to the plugin process\\n\\n4. **pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go** (`ClientV2.QueryData`): Marshals the request to protobuf format, sends it via gRPC, and converts the protobuf response back to the backend type using `backend.FromProto().QueryDataResponse()`\\n\\n5. **pkg/plugins/backendplugin/coreplugin/core_plugin.go** (`corePlugin.QueryData`): For in-process core plugins, directly invokes the query handler\\n\\n## Plugin Context Provider\\n**pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/plugincontext.go** provides the plugin context (datasource settings, user info, org ID, etc.) needed for query execution through `Get()` and related methods.\\n\\n## Plugin Middleware Chain\\nBefore execution, the query request passes through middleware in **pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/**:\\n- `logger_middleware.go`: Request/response logging\\n- `metrics_middleware.go`: Instrumentation and metrics collection\\n- `tracing_middleware.go`: OpenTelemetry tracing\\n- `httpclient_middleware.go`: HTTP header management\\n- `cookies_middleware.go`: Cookie handling\\n- `oauthtoken_middleware.go`: OAuth token injection\\n- `usealertingheaders_middleware.go`: Alerting-specific headers\\n\\n## Datasource-Specific Query Handlers\\nIndividual datasources implement `backend.QueryDataHandler` interface:\\n- **pkg/tsdb/loki/loki.go**: `Service.QueryData` executes LogQL queries\\n- **pkg/tsdb/prometheus/prometheus.go**: Executes PromQL queries via promlib\\n- **pkg/tsdb/graphite/graphite.go**: Executes Graphite metric queries\\n- **pkg/tsdb/cloudwatch/cloudwatch.go**: AWS CloudWatch metrics and logs\\n- **pkg/tsdb/tempo/tempo.go**: Trace queries\\n- **pkg/tsdb/jaeger/querydata.go**: Jaeger trace queries\\n- **pkg/tsdb/zipkin/handler_querydata.go**: Zipkin trace queries\\n- **pkg/tsdb/parca/plugin.go** & **pkg/tsdb/parca/service.go**: Profiling queries\\n\\n## Query Response Transformation\\nResponses are transformed back through the chain:\\n- Individual datasources create `backend.QueryDataResponse` containing frames\\n- Response passes back through middleware\\n- Plugin client converts protobuf responses\\n- Query service aggregates responses\\n- Frontend receives transformed data via **packages/grafana-runtime/src/utils/queryResponse.ts** `toDataQueryResponse()`\\n\\n## Alternative Routes\\n1. **Aggregator API Path** (**pkg/aggregator/apiserver/plugin/query.go**): Direct plugin query execution with `QueryDataHandler()` for Kubernetes-based deployments\\n\\n2. **Kubernetes Registry API** (**pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go**): REST API for query execution with object conversion via **pkg/registry/apis/datasource/queryconvert.go**\\n\\nThe entire flow implements the backend.QueryDataHandler interface at multiple levels, allowing for composable middleware, proper error handling, instrumentation, and support for both in-process and out-of-process plugin execution.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":8381,"cache_read_input_tokens":111707,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":8381},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"1b3f3d25-b7b1-496b-80c1-8a960f5a4928","uuid":"4fb88dc0-b5a0-4d8e-88b8-cd2e80647370"}
